<script language="JavaScript">
<!--Tips-->
var tipsTimerID;function showTips(nm){tipsTimerID = setTimeout(function(){var style=document.getElementById?document.getElementById(nm).style:(document.all?document.all(nm).style:(document.layers?document.layers[nm]:null));if(style) style.visibility='inherit';},500);}function hideTips(nm){clearTimeout(tipsTimerID);var style=document.getElementById?document.getElementById(nm).style:(document.all?document.all(nm).style:(document.layers?document.layers[nm]:null));if(style) style.visibility='hidden';}
<!--OpenClosePort-->
function port_open(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function port_close(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
<!--OpenCloseSet-->
function set_open(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function set_close(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
function jump(s){location.href = "/history/?code="+s;}
function showOtherMarket(){
    var otherMarket = document.getElementById('ulOtherMarket');
    if (otherMarket) {
        if (otherMarket.style.display == 'none') {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'block';
        } else {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'none';
        }
    }
}
function overAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add hover";
    }
}
function outAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
function downAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add down";
    }
}
function upAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
(function(){
    var marketSelect = document.getElementById('ddMarketSelect');
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (marketSelect) {
        try {
            marketSelect.addEventListener('click', showOtherMarket, false);
        } catch (e) {
            marketSelect.attachEvent('onclick', showOtherMarket);
        }
    }
    if (addPortfolio) {
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseover', overAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseover', overAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseout', outAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseout', outAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mousedown', downAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', downAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseup', upAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', upAddPortfolioButton);
        }
    }
})();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" src="https://s.yimg.jp/images/finance/js/yui/2.9.0/yahoo-dom-event.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://s.yimg.jp/images/finance/js/yui/2.9.0/calendar-min.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
YAHOO.util.Event.onDOMReady(function(){
    var marginFlg=false;
    var Event=YAHOO.util.Event,Dom=YAHOO.util.Dom,fdialog,fcalendar,tdialog,tcalendar;
    var fshowBtn=Dom.get("show"),fySel=Dom.get("selYear"),fmSel=Dom.get("selMonth"),fdSel=Dom.get("selDay"),
        tshowBtn=Dom.get("showT"),tySel=Dom.get("selYearT"),tmSel=Dom.get("selMonthT"),tdSel=Dom.get("selDayT");
    if (!marginFlg){
        var mTmRadio=Dom.get("monthly"),wTmRadio=Dom.get("weekly"),dTmRadio=Dom.get("daily");
    }
    function Cal(){this.showBtn,this.dialog,this.calendar,this.ySel,this.mSel,this.dSel,this.id;}
    var fCal=new Cal();fCal.showBtn=fshowBtn;fCal.dialog=fdialog;fCal.calendar=fcalendar;fCal.ySel=fySel;fCal.mSel=fmSel;fCal.dSel=fdSel;fCal.id="cal";
    var tCal=new Cal();tCal.showBtn=tshowBtn;tCal.dialog=tdialog;tCal.calendar=tcalendar;tCal.ySel=tySel;tCal.mSel=tmSel;tCal.dSel=tdSel;tCal.id="calT";

    chgOpt(fCal);
    chgOpt(tCal);
    if (!marginFlg){
        chgOptTerm();
    }
    Event.on(fshowBtn,"click",function(){showCalendar(fCal);});
    Event.on(tshowBtn,"click",function(){showCalendar(tCal);});
    Event.on(fySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    Event.on(fmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    if (!marginFlg){
        Event.on(mTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(wTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(dTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
    }

    function showCalendar(Cal){
        if (!Cal.calendar) {
            var now=new Date();
            Cal.calendar=new YAHOO.widget.CalendarGroup("calendar",Cal.id,{
                pages:2,
                title:"期間を指定してください",
                close:true,
                iframe:false,
                hide_blank_weeks:true,
                start_weekday:1,
                mindate:"01/01/1983",
                maxdate:now
            });
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_DAY_POSITION",3);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_SHORT",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_LONG",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_1CHAR",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_SHORT",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_MEDIUM",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_LONG",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_SUFFIX","\u5E74");
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_SUFFIX","");

            Cal.calendar.selectEvent.subscribe(function(){
                if(Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates().length>0){
                    var selDate=Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates()[0];
                    Cal.ySel.value=selDate.getFullYear();
                    Cal.mSel.value=selDate.getMonth()+1;
                    chgOpt(Cal);
                    Cal.dSel.value=selDate.getDate();
                }
                Cal.calendar.hide();
            });

            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
        } else {
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
            Cal.calendar.show();
        }
    }

    function chgOptTerm(){
        if (mTmRadio.checked){fCal.dSel.disabled=true;tCal.dSel.disabled=true;}
        else {fCal.dSel.disabled=false;tCal.dSel.disabled=false;chgOpt(fCal);chgOpt(tCal);}
    }

    function chgOpt(Cal){
        var cYear=2020,cMonth=12,cDay=4;
        var eom=31,dLen=Cal.dSel.length,mLen=Cal.mSel.length;
        if(Cal.mSel.value==2)eom=((Cal.ySel.value%4==0&&Cal.ySel.value%100!=0)||Cal.ySel.value%400==0)?29:28;
        else if(Cal.mSel.value==4||Cal.mSel.value==6||Cal.mSel.value==9||Cal.mSel.value==11)eom=30;
        if(Cal.ySel.value==cYear){
            while(Cal.mSel[cMonth]!=null){Cal.mSel[cMonth]=null;}
            if(Cal.mSel.value==cMonth)while(Cal.dSel[cDay]!=null){Cal.dSel[cDay]=null;}
            else if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }else{
            if(mLen<12)for(i=mLen;i<12;i++){Cal.mSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
            if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }
    }
});
</script>

<script language="JavaScript">
<!--Tips-->
var tipsTimerID;function showTips(nm){tipsTimerID = setTimeout(function(){var style=document.getElementById?document.getElementById(nm).style:(document.all?document.all(nm).style:(document.layers?document.layers[nm]:null));if(style) style.visibility='inherit';},500);}function hideTips(nm){clearTimeout(tipsTimerID);var style=document.getElementById?document.getElementById(nm).style:(document.all?document.all(nm).style:(document.layers?document.layers[nm]:null));if(style) style.visibility='hidden';}
<!--OpenClosePort-->
function port_open(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function port_close(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
<!--OpenCloseSet-->
function set_open(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function set_close(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
function jump(s){location.href = "/history/?code="+s;}
function showOtherMarket(){
    var otherMarket = document.getElementById('ulOtherMarket');
    if (otherMarket) {
        if (otherMarket.style.display == 'none') {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'block';
        } else {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'none';
        }
    }
}
function overAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add hover";
    }
}
function outAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
function downAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add down";
    }
}
function upAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
(function(){
    var marketSelect = document.getElementById('ddMarketSelect');
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (marketSelect) {
        try {
            marketSelect.addEventListener('click', showOtherMarket, false);
        } catch (e) {
            marketSelect.attachEvent('onclick', showOtherMarket);
        }
    }
    if (addPortfolio) {
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseover', overAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseover', overAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseout', outAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseout', outAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mousedown', downAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', downAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseup', upAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', upAddPortfolioButton);
        }
    }
})();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" src="https://s.yimg.jp/images/finance/js/yui/2.9.0/yahoo-dom-event.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://s.yimg.jp/images/finance/js/yui/2.9.0/calendar-min.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
YAHOO.util.Event.onDOMReady(function(){
    var marginFlg=false;
    var Event=YAHOO.util.Event,Dom=YAHOO.util.Dom,fdialog,fcalendar,tdialog,tcalendar;
    var fshowBtn=Dom.get("show"),fySel=Dom.get("selYear"),fmSel=Dom.get("selMonth"),fdSel=Dom.get("selDay"),
        tshowBtn=Dom.get("showT"),tySel=Dom.get("selYearT"),tmSel=Dom.get("selMonthT"),tdSel=Dom.get("selDayT");
    if (!marginFlg){
        var mTmRadio=Dom.get("monthly"),wTmRadio=Dom.get("weekly"),dTmRadio=Dom.get("daily");
    }
    function Cal(){this.showBtn,this.dialog,this.calendar,this.ySel,this.mSel,this.dSel,this.id;}
    var fCal=new Cal();fCal.showBtn=fshowBtn;fCal.dialog=fdialog;fCal.calendar=fcalendar;fCal.ySel=fySel;fCal.mSel=fmSel;fCal.dSel=fdSel;fCal.id="cal";
    var tCal=new Cal();tCal.showBtn=tshowBtn;tCal.dialog=tdialog;tCal.calendar=tcalendar;tCal.ySel=tySel;tCal.mSel=tmSel;tCal.dSel=tdSel;tCal.id="calT";

    chgOpt(fCal);
    chgOpt(tCal);
    if (!marginFlg){
        chgOptTerm();
    }
    Event.on(fshowBtn,"click",function(){showCalendar(fCal);});
    Event.on(tshowBtn,"click",function(){showCalendar(tCal);});
    Event.on(fySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    Event.on(fmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    if (!marginFlg){
        Event.on(mTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(wTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(dTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
    }

    function showCalendar(Cal){
        if (!Cal.calendar) {
            var now=new Date();
            Cal.calendar=new YAHOO.widget.CalendarGroup("calendar",Cal.id,{
                pages:2,
                title:"期間を指定してください",
                close:true,
                iframe:false,
                hide_blank_weeks:true,
                start_weekday:1,
                mindate:"01/01/1983",
                maxdate:now
            });
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_DAY_POSITION",3);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_SHORT",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_LONG",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_1CHAR",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_SHORT",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_MEDIUM",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_LONG",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_SUFFIX","\u5E74");
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_SUFFIX","");

            Cal.calendar.selectEvent.subscribe(function(){
                if(Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates().length>0){
                    var selDate=Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates()[0];
                    Cal.ySel.value=selDate.getFullYear();
                    Cal.mSel.value=selDate.getMonth()+1;
                    chgOpt(Cal);
                    Cal.dSel.value=selDate.getDate();
                }
                Cal.calendar.hide();
            });

            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
        } else {
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
            Cal.calendar.show();
        }
    }

    function chgOptTerm(){
        if (mTmRadio.checked){fCal.dSel.disabled=true;tCal.dSel.disabled=true;}
        else {fCal.dSel.disabled=false;tCal.dSel.disabled=false;chgOpt(fCal);chgOpt(tCal);}
    }

    function chgOpt(Cal){
        var cYear=2020,cMonth=12,cDay=4;
        var eom=31,dLen=Cal.dSel.length,mLen=Cal.mSel.length;
        if(Cal.mSel.value==2)eom=((Cal.ySel.value%4==0&&Cal.ySel.value%100!=0)||Cal.ySel.value%400==0)?29:28;
        else if(Cal.mSel.value==4||Cal.mSel.value==6||Cal.mSel.value==9||Cal.mSel.value==11)eom=30;
        if(Cal.ySel.value==cYear){
            while(Cal.mSel[cMonth]!=null){Cal.mSel[cMonth]=null;}
            if(Cal.mSel.value==cMonth)while(Cal.dSel[cDay]!=null){Cal.dSel[cDay]=null;}
            else if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }else{
            if(mLen<12)for(i=mLen;i<12;i++){Cal.mSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
            if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }
    }
});
</script>

function port_open(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function port_close(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
<!--OpenCloseSet-->
function set_open(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function set_close(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
function jump(s){location.href = "/history/?code="+s;}
function showOtherMarket(){
    var otherMarket = document.getElementById('ulOtherMarket');
    if (otherMarket) {
        if (otherMarket.style.display == 'none') {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'block';
        } else {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'none';
        }
    }
}
function overAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add hover";
    }
}
function outAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
function downAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add down";
    }
}
function upAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
(function(){
    var marketSelect = document.getElementById('ddMarketSelect');
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (marketSelect) {
        try {
            marketSelect.addEventListener('click', showOtherMarket, false);
        } catch (e) {
            marketSelect.attachEvent('onclick', showOtherMarket);
        }
    }
    if (addPortfolio) {
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseover', overAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseover', overAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseout', outAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseout', outAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mousedown', downAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', downAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseup', upAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', upAddPortfolioButton);
        }
    }
})();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" src="https://s.yimg.jp/images/finance/js/yui/2.9.0/yahoo-dom-event.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://s.yimg.jp/images/finance/js/yui/2.9.0/calendar-min.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
YAHOO.util.Event.onDOMReady(function(){
    var marginFlg=false;
    var Event=YAHOO.util.Event,Dom=YAHOO.util.Dom,fdialog,fcalendar,tdialog,tcalendar;
    var fshowBtn=Dom.get("show"),fySel=Dom.get("selYear"),fmSel=Dom.get("selMonth"),fdSel=Dom.get("selDay"),
        tshowBtn=Dom.get("showT"),tySel=Dom.get("selYearT"),tmSel=Dom.get("selMonthT"),tdSel=Dom.get("selDayT");
    if (!marginFlg){
        var mTmRadio=Dom.get("monthly"),wTmRadio=Dom.get("weekly"),dTmRadio=Dom.get("daily");
    }
    function Cal(){this.showBtn,this.dialog,this.calendar,this.ySel,this.mSel,this.dSel,this.id;}
    var fCal=new Cal();fCal.showBtn=fshowBtn;fCal.dialog=fdialog;fCal.calendar=fcalendar;fCal.ySel=fySel;fCal.mSel=fmSel;fCal.dSel=fdSel;fCal.id="cal";
    var tCal=new Cal();tCal.showBtn=tshowBtn;tCal.dialog=tdialog;tCal.calendar=tcalendar;tCal.ySel=tySel;tCal.mSel=tmSel;tCal.dSel=tdSel;tCal.id="calT";

    chgOpt(fCal);
    chgOpt(tCal);
    if (!marginFlg){
        chgOptTerm();
    }
    Event.on(fshowBtn,"click",function(){showCalendar(fCal);});
    Event.on(tshowBtn,"click",function(){showCalendar(tCal);});
    Event.on(fySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    Event.on(fmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    if (!marginFlg){
        Event.on(mTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(wTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(dTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
    }

    function showCalendar(Cal){
        if (!Cal.calendar) {
            var now=new Date();
            Cal.calendar=new YAHOO.widget.CalendarGroup("calendar",Cal.id,{
                pages:2,
                title:"期間を指定してください",
                close:true,
                iframe:false,
                hide_blank_weeks:true,
                start_weekday:1,
                mindate:"01/01/1983",
                maxdate:now
            });
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_DAY_POSITION",3);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_SHORT",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_LONG",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_1CHAR",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_SHORT",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_MEDIUM",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_LONG",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_SUFFIX","\u5E74");
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_SUFFIX","");

            Cal.calendar.selectEvent.subscribe(function(){
                if(Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates().length>0){
                    var selDate=Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates()[0];
                    Cal.ySel.value=selDate.getFullYear();
                    Cal.mSel.value=selDate.getMonth()+1;
                    chgOpt(Cal);
                    Cal.dSel.value=selDate.getDate();
                }
                Cal.calendar.hide();
            });

            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
        } else {
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
            Cal.calendar.show();
        }
    }

    function chgOptTerm(){
        if (mTmRadio.checked){fCal.dSel.disabled=true;tCal.dSel.disabled=true;}
        else {fCal.dSel.disabled=false;tCal.dSel.disabled=false;chgOpt(fCal);chgOpt(tCal);}
    }

    function chgOpt(Cal){
        var cYear=2020,cMonth=12,cDay=4;
        var eom=31,dLen=Cal.dSel.length,mLen=Cal.mSel.length;
        if(Cal.mSel.value==2)eom=((Cal.ySel.value%4==0&&Cal.ySel.value%100!=0)||Cal.ySel.value%400==0)?29:28;
        else if(Cal.mSel.value==4||Cal.mSel.value==6||Cal.mSel.value==9||Cal.mSel.value==11)eom=30;
        if(Cal.ySel.value==cYear){
            while(Cal.mSel[cMonth]!=null){Cal.mSel[cMonth]=null;}
            if(Cal.mSel.value==cMonth)while(Cal.dSel[cDay]!=null){Cal.dSel[cDay]=null;}
            else if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }else{
            if(mLen<12)for(i=mLen;i<12;i++){Cal.mSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
            if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }
    }
});
</script>

<dd><em>・</em><span>年初来高値・安値は、1月1日から3月31日までは昨年来高値・安値（前年1月1日からの最高値・最安値）を表示しています。</span></dd>

<script language="JavaScript">
<!--Tips-->
var tipsTimerID;function showTips(nm){tipsTimerID = setTimeout(function(){var style=document.getElementById?document.getElementById(nm).style:(document.all?document.all(nm).style:(document.layers?document.layers[nm]:null));if(style) style.visibility='inherit';},500);}function hideTips(nm){clearTimeout(tipsTimerID);var style=document.getElementById?document.getElementById(nm).style:(document.all?document.all(nm).style:(document.layers?document.layers[nm]:null));if(style) style.visibility='hidden';}
<!--OpenClosePort-->
function port_open(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function port_close(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
<!--OpenCloseSet-->
function set_open(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function set_close(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
function jump(s){location.href = "/history/?code="+s;}
function showOtherMarket(){
    var otherMarket = document.getElementById('ulOtherMarket');
    if (otherMarket) {
        if (otherMarket.style.display == 'none') {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'block';
        } else {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'none';
        }
    }
}
function overAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add hover";
    }
}
function outAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
function downAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add down";
    }
}
function upAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
(function(){
    var marketSelect = document.getElementById('ddMarketSelect');
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (marketSelect) {
        try {
            marketSelect.addEventListener('click', showOtherMarket, false);
        } catch (e) {
            marketSelect.attachEvent('onclick', showOtherMarket);
        }
    }
    if (addPortfolio) {
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseover', overAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseover', overAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseout', outAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseout', outAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mousedown', downAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', downAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseup', upAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', upAddPortfolioButton);
        }
    }
})();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" src="https://s.yimg.jp/images/finance/js/yui/2.9.0/yahoo-dom-event.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://s.yimg.jp/images/finance/js/yui/2.9.0/calendar-min.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
YAHOO.util.Event.onDOMReady(function(){
    var marginFlg=false;
    var Event=YAHOO.util.Event,Dom=YAHOO.util.Dom,fdialog,fcalendar,tdialog,tcalendar;
    var fshowBtn=Dom.get("show"),fySel=Dom.get("selYear"),fmSel=Dom.get("selMonth"),fdSel=Dom.get("selDay"),
        tshowBtn=Dom.get("showT"),tySel=Dom.get("selYearT"),tmSel=Dom.get("selMonthT"),tdSel=Dom.get("selDayT");
    if (!marginFlg){
        var mTmRadio=Dom.get("monthly"),wTmRadio=Dom.get("weekly"),dTmRadio=Dom.get("daily");
    }
    function Cal(){this.showBtn,this.dialog,this.calendar,this.ySel,this.mSel,this.dSel,this.id;}
    var fCal=new Cal();fCal.showBtn=fshowBtn;fCal.dialog=fdialog;fCal.calendar=fcalendar;fCal.ySel=fySel;fCal.mSel=fmSel;fCal.dSel=fdSel;fCal.id="cal";
    var tCal=new Cal();tCal.showBtn=tshowBtn;tCal.dialog=tdialog;tCal.calendar=tcalendar;tCal.ySel=tySel;tCal.mSel=tmSel;tCal.dSel=tdSel;tCal.id="calT";

    chgOpt(fCal);
    chgOpt(tCal);
    if (!marginFlg){
        chgOptTerm();
    }
    Event.on(fshowBtn,"click",function(){showCalendar(fCal);});
    Event.on(tshowBtn,"click",function(){showCalendar(tCal);});
    Event.on(fySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    Event.on(fmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    if (!marginFlg){
        Event.on(mTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(wTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(dTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
    }

    function showCalendar(Cal){
        if (!Cal.calendar) {
            var now=new Date();
            Cal.calendar=new YAHOO.widget.CalendarGroup("calendar",Cal.id,{
                pages:2,
                title:"期間を指定してください",
                close:true,
                iframe:false,
                hide_blank_weeks:true,
                start_weekday:1,
                mindate:"01/01/1983",
                maxdate:now
            });
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_DAY_POSITION",3);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_SHORT",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_LONG",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_1CHAR",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_SHORT",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_MEDIUM",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_LONG",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_SUFFIX","\u5E74");
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_SUFFIX","");

            Cal.calendar.selectEvent.subscribe(function(){
                if(Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates().length>0){
                    var selDate=Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates()[0];
                    Cal.ySel.value=selDate.getFullYear();
                    Cal.mSel.value=selDate.getMonth()+1;
                    chgOpt(Cal);
                    Cal.dSel.value=selDate.getDate();
                }
                Cal.calendar.hide();
            });

            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
        } else {
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
            Cal.calendar.show();
        }
    }

    function chgOptTerm(){
        if (mTmRadio.checked){fCal.dSel.disabled=true;tCal.dSel.disabled=true;}
        else {fCal.dSel.disabled=false;tCal.dSel.disabled=false;chgOpt(fCal);chgOpt(tCal);}
    }

    function chgOpt(Cal){
        var cYear=2020,cMonth=12,cDay=4;
        var eom=31,dLen=Cal.dSel.length,mLen=Cal.mSel.length;
        if(Cal.mSel.value==2)eom=((Cal.ySel.value%4==0&&Cal.ySel.value%100!=0)||Cal.ySel.value%400==0)?29:28;
        else if(Cal.mSel.value==4||Cal.mSel.value==6||Cal.mSel.value==9||Cal.mSel.value==11)eom=30;
        if(Cal.ySel.value==cYear){
            while(Cal.mSel[cMonth]!=null){Cal.mSel[cMonth]=null;}
            if(Cal.mSel.value==cMonth)while(Cal.dSel[cDay]!=null){Cal.dSel[cDay]=null;}
            else if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }else{
            if(mLen<12)for(i=mLen;i<12;i++){Cal.mSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
            if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }
    }
});
</script>

<script language="JavaScript">
<!--Tips-->
var tipsTimerID;function showTips(nm){tipsTimerID = setTimeout(function(){var style=document.getElementById?document.getElementById(nm).style:(document.all?document.all(nm).style:(document.layers?document.layers[nm]:null));if(style) style.visibility='inherit';},500);}function hideTips(nm){clearTimeout(tipsTimerID);var style=document.getElementById?document.getElementById(nm).style:(document.all?document.all(nm).style:(document.layers?document.layers[nm]:null));if(style) style.visibility='hidden';}
<!--OpenClosePort-->
function port_open(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function port_close(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
<!--OpenCloseSet-->
function set_open(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function set_close(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
function jump(s){location.href = "/history/?code="+s;}
function showOtherMarket(){
    var otherMarket = document.getElementById('ulOtherMarket');
    if (otherMarket) {
        if (otherMarket.style.display == 'none') {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'block';
        } else {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'none';
        }
    }
}
function overAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add hover";
    }
}
function outAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
function downAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add down";
    }
}
function upAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
(function(){
    var marketSelect = document.getElementById('ddMarketSelect');
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (marketSelect) {
        try {
            marketSelect.addEventListener('click', showOtherMarket, false);
        } catch (e) {
            marketSelect.attachEvent('onclick', showOtherMarket);
        }
    }
    if (addPortfolio) {
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseover', overAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseover', overAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseout', outAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseout', outAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mousedown', downAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', downAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseup', upAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', upAddPortfolioButton);
        }
    }
})();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" src="https://s.yimg.jp/images/finance/js/yui/2.9.0/yahoo-dom-event.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://s.yimg.jp/images/finance/js/yui/2.9.0/calendar-min.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
YAHOO.util.Event.onDOMReady(function(){
    var marginFlg=false;
    var Event=YAHOO.util.Event,Dom=YAHOO.util.Dom,fdialog,fcalendar,tdialog,tcalendar;
    var fshowBtn=Dom.get("show"),fySel=Dom.get("selYear"),fmSel=Dom.get("selMonth"),fdSel=Dom.get("selDay"),
        tshowBtn=Dom.get("showT"),tySel=Dom.get("selYearT"),tmSel=Dom.get("selMonthT"),tdSel=Dom.get("selDayT");
    if (!marginFlg){
        var mTmRadio=Dom.get("monthly"),wTmRadio=Dom.get("weekly"),dTmRadio=Dom.get("daily");
    }
    function Cal(){this.showBtn,this.dialog,this.calendar,this.ySel,this.mSel,this.dSel,this.id;}
    var fCal=new Cal();fCal.showBtn=fshowBtn;fCal.dialog=fdialog;fCal.calendar=fcalendar;fCal.ySel=fySel;fCal.mSel=fmSel;fCal.dSel=fdSel;fCal.id="cal";
    var tCal=new Cal();tCal.showBtn=tshowBtn;tCal.dialog=tdialog;tCal.calendar=tcalendar;tCal.ySel=tySel;tCal.mSel=tmSel;tCal.dSel=tdSel;tCal.id="calT";

    chgOpt(fCal);
    chgOpt(tCal);
    if (!marginFlg){
        chgOptTerm();
    }
    Event.on(fshowBtn,"click",function(){showCalendar(fCal);});
    Event.on(tshowBtn,"click",function(){showCalendar(tCal);});
    Event.on(fySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    Event.on(fmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    if (!marginFlg){
        Event.on(mTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(wTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(dTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
    }

    function showCalendar(Cal){
        if (!Cal.calendar) {
            var now=new Date();
            Cal.calendar=new YAHOO.widget.CalendarGroup("calendar",Cal.id,{
                pages:2,
                title:"期間を指定してください",
                close:true,
                iframe:false,
                hide_blank_weeks:true,
                start_weekday:1,
                mindate:"01/01/1983",
                maxdate:now
            });
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_DAY_POSITION",3);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_SHORT",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_LONG",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_1CHAR",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_SHORT",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_MEDIUM",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_LONG",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_SUFFIX","\u5E74");
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_SUFFIX","");

            Cal.calendar.selectEvent.subscribe(function(){
                if(Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates().length>0){
                    var selDate=Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates()[0];
                    Cal.ySel.value=selDate.getFullYear();
                    Cal.mSel.value=selDate.getMonth()+1;
                    chgOpt(Cal);
                    Cal.dSel.value=selDate.getDate();
                }
                Cal.calendar.hide();
            });

            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
        } else {
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
            Cal.calendar.show();
        }
    }

    function chgOptTerm(){
        if (mTmRadio.checked){fCal.dSel.disabled=true;tCal.dSel.disabled=true;}
        else {fCal.dSel.disabled=false;tCal.dSel.disabled=false;chgOpt(fCal);chgOpt(tCal);}
    }

    function chgOpt(Cal){
        var cYear=2020,cMonth=12,cDay=4;
        var eom=31,dLen=Cal.dSel.length,mLen=Cal.mSel.length;
        if(Cal.mSel.value==2)eom=((Cal.ySel.value%4==0&&Cal.ySel.value%100!=0)||Cal.ySel.value%400==0)?29:28;
        else if(Cal.mSel.value==4||Cal.mSel.value==6||Cal.mSel.value==9||Cal.mSel.value==11)eom=30;
        if(Cal.ySel.value==cYear){
            while(Cal.mSel[cMonth]!=null){Cal.mSel[cMonth]=null;}
            if(Cal.mSel.value==cMonth)while(Cal.dSel[cDay]!=null){Cal.dSel[cDay]=null;}
            else if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }else{
            if(mLen<12)for(i=mLen;i<12;i++){Cal.mSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
            if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }
    }
});
</script>

<script language="JavaScript">
<!--Tips-->
var tipsTimerID;function showTips(nm){tipsTimerID = setTimeout(function(){var style=document.getElementById?document.getElementById(nm).style:(document.all?document.all(nm).style:(document.layers?document.layers[nm]:null));if(style) style.visibility='inherit';},500);}function hideTips(nm){clearTimeout(tipsTimerID);var style=document.getElementById?document.getElementById(nm).style:(document.all?document.all(nm).style:(document.layers?document.layers[nm]:null));if(style) style.visibility='hidden';}
<!--OpenClosePort-->
function port_open(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function port_close(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
<!--OpenCloseSet-->
function set_open(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function set_close(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
function jump(s){location.href = "/history/?code="+s;}
function showOtherMarket(){
    var otherMarket = document.getElementById('ulOtherMarket');
    if (otherMarket) {
        if (otherMarket.style.display == 'none') {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'block';
        } else {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'none';
        }
    }
}
function overAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add hover";
    }
}
function outAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
function downAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add down";
    }
}
function upAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
(function(){
    var marketSelect = document.getElementById('ddMarketSelect');
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (marketSelect) {
        try {
            marketSelect.addEventListener('click', showOtherMarket, false);
        } catch (e) {
            marketSelect.attachEvent('onclick', showOtherMarket);
        }
    }
    if (addPortfolio) {
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseover', overAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseover', overAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseout', outAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseout', outAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mousedown', downAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', downAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseup', upAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', upAddPortfolioButton);
        }
    }
})();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" src="https://s.yimg.jp/images/finance/js/yui/2.9.0/yahoo-dom-event.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://s.yimg.jp/images/finance/js/yui/2.9.0/calendar-min.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
YAHOO.util.Event.onDOMReady(function(){
    var marginFlg=false;
    var Event=YAHOO.util.Event,Dom=YAHOO.util.Dom,fdialog,fcalendar,tdialog,tcalendar;
    var fshowBtn=Dom.get("show"),fySel=Dom.get("selYear"),fmSel=Dom.get("selMonth"),fdSel=Dom.get("selDay"),
        tshowBtn=Dom.get("showT"),tySel=Dom.get("selYearT"),tmSel=Dom.get("selMonthT"),tdSel=Dom.get("selDayT");
    if (!marginFlg){
        var mTmRadio=Dom.get("monthly"),wTmRadio=Dom.get("weekly"),dTmRadio=Dom.get("daily");
    }
    function Cal(){this.showBtn,this.dialog,this.calendar,this.ySel,this.mSel,this.dSel,this.id;}
    var fCal=new Cal();fCal.showBtn=fshowBtn;fCal.dialog=fdialog;fCal.calendar=fcalendar;fCal.ySel=fySel;fCal.mSel=fmSel;fCal.dSel=fdSel;fCal.id="cal";
    var tCal=new Cal();tCal.showBtn=tshowBtn;tCal.dialog=tdialog;tCal.calendar=tcalendar;tCal.ySel=tySel;tCal.mSel=tmSel;tCal.dSel=tdSel;tCal.id="calT";

    chgOpt(fCal);
    chgOpt(tCal);
    if (!marginFlg){
        chgOptTerm();
    }
    Event.on(fshowBtn,"click",function(){showCalendar(fCal);});
    Event.on(tshowBtn,"click",function(){showCalendar(tCal);});
    Event.on(fySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    Event.on(fmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    if (!marginFlg){
        Event.on(mTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(wTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(dTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
    }

    function showCalendar(Cal){
        if (!Cal.calendar) {
            var now=new Date();
            Cal.calendar=new YAHOO.widget.CalendarGroup("calendar",Cal.id,{
                pages:2,
                title:"期間を指定してください",
                close:true,
                iframe:false,
                hide_blank_weeks:true,
                start_weekday:1,
                mindate:"01/01/1983",
                maxdate:now
            });
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_DAY_POSITION",3);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_SHORT",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_LONG",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_1CHAR",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_SHORT",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_MEDIUM",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_LONG",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_SUFFIX","\u5E74");
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_SUFFIX","");

            Cal.calendar.selectEvent.subscribe(function(){
                if(Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates().length>0){
                    var selDate=Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates()[0];
                    Cal.ySel.value=selDate.getFullYear();
                    Cal.mSel.value=selDate.getMonth()+1;
                    chgOpt(Cal);
                    Cal.dSel.value=selDate.getDate();
                }
                Cal.calendar.hide();
            });

            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
        } else {
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
            Cal.calendar.show();
        }
    }

    function chgOptTerm(){
        if (mTmRadio.checked){fCal.dSel.disabled=true;tCal.dSel.disabled=true;}
        else {fCal.dSel.disabled=false;tCal.dSel.disabled=false;chgOpt(fCal);chgOpt(tCal);}
    }

    function chgOpt(Cal){
        var cYear=2020,cMonth=12,cDay=4;
        var eom=31,dLen=Cal.dSel.length,mLen=Cal.mSel.length;
        if(Cal.mSel.value==2)eom=((Cal.ySel.value%4==0&&Cal.ySel.value%100!=0)||Cal.ySel.value%400==0)?29:28;
        else if(Cal.mSel.value==4||Cal.mSel.value==6||Cal.mSel.value==9||Cal.mSel.value==11)eom=30;
        if(Cal.ySel.value==cYear){
            while(Cal.mSel[cMonth]!=null){Cal.mSel[cMonth]=null;}
            if(Cal.mSel.value==cMonth)while(Cal.dSel[cDay]!=null){Cal.dSel[cDay]=null;}
            else if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }else{
            if(mLen<12)for(i=mLen;i<12;i++){Cal.mSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
            if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }
    }
});
</script>

<div class="stocksHistoryNotice yjSt">
<dl>
<dt>【時系列について】</dt>
<dd><em>*</em><span>分割による調整については「<a href="https://www.yahoo-help.jp/app/answers/detail/p/546/a_id/45316">調整後終値とは</a>」を参照してください。</span></dd>
<dd><em>・</em><span>信用残時系列データは、信用銘柄でない場合、表示されません。</span></dd>
<dd><em>・</em><span>信用残時系列データは、週1回の発表で、金曜日時点のデータを翌週火曜日に更新します(祝日などにより変動することがあります)。</span></dd>
<dd><em>・</em><span>年初来高値・安値は、1月1日から3月31日までは昨年来高値・安値（前年1月1日からの最高値・最安値）を表示しています。</span></dd>
<dd><em>・</em><span>用語の意味については「<a href="https://www.yahoo-help.jp/app/answers/detail/p/546/a_id/45275">ファイナンス用語集</a>」「<a href="https://info.finance.yahoo.co.jp/dictionary/">信用残データ関連用語</a>」をご覧ください。</span></dd>
<dd><em>・</em><span>時系列データは東京証券取引所 ・ 大阪取引所 ・ 名古屋証券取引所 ・ 野村総合研究所 ・ モーニングスター ・ リフィニティブ・ジャパンからの提供を受けています。</span></dd>

<!--Tips-->
var tipsTimerID;function showTips(nm){tipsTimerID = setTimeout(function(){var style=document.getElementById?document.getElementById(nm).style:(document.all?document.all(nm).style:(document.layers?document.layers[nm]:null));if(style) style.visibility='inherit';},500);}function hideTips(nm){clearTimeout(tipsTimerID);var style=document.getElementById?document.getElementById(nm).style:(document.all?document.all(nm).style:(document.layers?document.layers[nm]:null));if(style) style.visibility='hidden';}
<!--OpenClosePort-->
function port_open(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function port_close(){if(document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('portVisible').style.display = 'none';document.getElementById('btnValueOpen').style.display = 'block';document.getElementById('btnValueClose').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
<!--OpenCloseSet-->
function set_open(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'none'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'block';return false;}}function set_close(){if(document.getElementById('setModule').style.display == 'block'){document.getElementById('setModule').style.display = 'none';return false;}}
function jump(s){location.href = "/history/?code="+s;}
function showOtherMarket(){
    var otherMarket = document.getElementById('ulOtherMarket');
    if (otherMarket) {
        if (otherMarket.style.display == 'none') {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'block';
        } else {
            otherMarket.style.display = 'none';
        }
    }
}
function overAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add hover";
    }
}
function outAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
function downAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add down";
    }
}
function upAddPortfolioButton() {
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (addPortfolio) {
        addPortfolio.className = "add";
    }
}
(function(){
    var marketSelect = document.getElementById('ddMarketSelect');
    var addPortfolio = document.getElementById('divAddPortfolio');
    if (marketSelect) {
        try {
            marketSelect.addEventListener('click', showOtherMarket, false);
        } catch (e) {
            marketSelect.attachEvent('onclick', showOtherMarket);
        }
    }
    if (addPortfolio) {
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseover', overAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseover', overAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseout', outAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onmouseout', outAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mousedown', downAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', downAddPortfolioButton);
        }
        try {
            addPortfolio.addEventListener('mouseup', upAddPortfolioButton, false);
        } catch (e) {
            addPortfolio.attachEvent('onclick', upAddPortfolioButton);
        }
    }
})();
</script>

        chgOptTerm();
    }

    Event.on(tshowBtn,"click",function(){showCalendar(tCal);});
    Event.on(fySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tySel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    Event.on(fmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(fCal);});
    Event.on(tmSel,"change",function(){chgOpt(tCal);});
    if (!marginFlg){
        Event.on(mTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(wTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
        Event.on(dTmRadio,"click",function(){chgOptTerm();});
    }

    function showCalendar(Cal){
        if (!Cal.calendar) {
            var now=new Date();
            Cal.calendar=new YAHOO.widget.CalendarGroup("calendar",Cal.id,{
                pages:2,
                title:"期間を指定してください",
                close:true,
                iframe:false,
                hide_blank_weeks:true,
                start_weekday:1,
                mindate:"01/01/1983",
                maxdate:now
            });
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MDY_DAY_POSITION",3);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_SHORT",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MONTHS_LONG",["1\u6708","2\u6708","3\u6708","4\u6708","5\u6708","6\u6708","7\u6708","8\u6708","9\u6708","10\u6708","11\u6708","12\u6708"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_1CHAR",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_SHORT",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_MEDIUM",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("WEEKDAYS_LONG",["\u65E5","\u6708","\u706B","\u6C34","\u6728","\u91D1","\u571F"]);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_POSITION",1);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_POSITION",2);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_YEAR_SUFFIX","\u5E74");
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("MY_LABEL_MONTH_SUFFIX","");

            Cal.calendar.selectEvent.subscribe(function(){
                if(Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates().length>0){
                    var selDate=Cal.calendar.getSelectedDates()[0];
                    Cal.ySel.value=selDate.getFullYear();
                    Cal.mSel.value=selDate.getMonth()+1;
                    chgOpt(Cal);
                    Cal.dSel.value=selDate.getDate();
                }
                Cal.calendar.hide();
            });

            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
        } else {
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("PAGEDATE",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.cfg.setProperty("SELECTED",Cal.ySel.value+"/"+Cal.mSel.value+"/"+Cal.dSel.value);
            Cal.calendar.render();
            Cal.calendar.show();
        }
    }

    function chgOptTerm(){
        if (mTmRadio.checked){fCal.dSel.disabled=true;tCal.dSel.disabled=true;}
        else {fCal.dSel.disabled=false;tCal.dSel.disabled=false;chgOpt(fCal);chgOpt(tCal);}
    }

    function chgOpt(Cal){
        var cYear=2020,cMonth=12,cDay=4;
        var eom=31,dLen=Cal.dSel.length,mLen=Cal.mSel.length;
        if(Cal.mSel.value==2)eom=((Cal.ySel.value%4==0&&Cal.ySel.value%100!=0)||Cal.ySel.value%400==0)?29:28;
        else if(Cal.mSel.value==4||Cal.mSel.value==6||Cal.mSel.value==9||Cal.mSel.value==11)eom=30;
        if(Cal.ySel.value==cYear){
            while(Cal.mSel[cMonth]!=null){Cal.mSel[cMonth]=null;}
            if(Cal.mSel.value==cMonth)while(Cal.dSel[cDay]!=null){Cal.dSel[cDay]=null;}
            else if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }else{
            if(mLen<12)for(i=mLen;i<12;i++){Cal.mSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
            if(dLen>eom)while(Cal.dSel[eom]!=null){Cal.dSel[eom]=null;}
            else if(dLen<eom)for(i=dLen;i<eom;i++){Cal.dSel[i]=new Option(i+1,i+1);}
        }
    }
});
</script>
